<span></span>

Coffs Harbour Seventh-day Adventist Church, located in the picturesque coastal city of Coffs Harbour, NSW, serves as a welcoming 'church near me' for anyone seeking a spiritual home. Known for its friendly and diverse congregation, the church is committed to creating a supportive environment where individuals and families can explore their faith and grow together in their spiritual journeys. Offering a variety of worship experiences, Bible study groups, and youth programs, Coffs Harbour Seventh-day Adventist Church is dedicated to providing meaningful opportunities for connection, learning, and service. With a strong focus on community outreach, the church actively participates in initiatives aimed at improving the lives of those in need within the local and global community. Whether you're a long-time resident or new to the area, Coffs Harbour Seventh-day Adventist Church invites you to join their community of faith, fellowship, and service.

<p><span></span></p>
<p>Lightning Ridge Seventh-day Adventist Church, situated in the unique opal mining town of Lightning Ridge, NSW, offers a 'church near me' for those seeking a community of faith amidst the town's distinctive landscape. This church is renowned for its warm hospitality, providing a welcoming environment for both locals and visitors. With engaging worship services, Bible study sessions, and a strong emphasis on community outreach, Lightning Ridge Seventh-day Adventist Church aims to foster spiritual growth and a sense of belonging among its members. It's a place where individuals and families can explore their faith, participate in service opportunities, and build meaningful relationships. Whether you're drawn to Lightning Ridge for its gems or its charm, this church invites you to discover a spiritual home and community support within its congregation.</p>

Whether you're native Spanish-speaking or interested in the Spanish language and culture, this church invites you to join their family of believers in faith and friendship.
